<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Selected_works">Selected works</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mario_Vargas_Llosa&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Selected works">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em;">
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fiction">Fiction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mario_Vargas_Llosa&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Fiction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>1959 – <i>Los jefes</i> (<i><a href="/w/index.php?title=The_Cubs_and_Other_Stories&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="The Cubs and Other Stories (page does not exist)">The Cubs and Other Stories</a></i>, 1979)</li>
<li>1963 – <i>La ciudad y los perros</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Time_of_the_Hero" title="The Time of the Hero">The Time of the Hero</a></i>, 1966)</li>
<li>1966 – <i>La casa verde</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Green_House" title="The Green House">The Green House</a></i>, 1968)</li>
<li>1969 – <i>Conversación en la catedral</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/Conversation_in_the_Cathedral" title="Conversation in the Cathedral">Conversation in the Cathedral</a></i>, 1975)</li>
<li>1973 – <i>Pantaleón y las visitadoras</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/Captain_Pantoja_and_the_Special_Service" title="Captain Pantoja and the Special Service">Captain Pantoja and the Special Service</a></i>, 1978)</li>
<li>1977 – <i>La tía Julia y el escribidor</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/Aunt_Julia_and_the_Scriptwriter" title="Aunt Julia and the Scriptwriter">Aunt Julia and the Scriptwriter</a></i>, 1982)</li>
<li>1981 – <i>La guerra del fin del mundo</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_War_of_the_End_of_the_World" title="The War of the End of the World">The War of the End of the World</a></i>, 1984)</li>
<li>1984 – <i>Historia de Mayta</i> (<i>The Real Life of Alejandro Mayta</i>, 1985)</li>
<li>1986 – <i>¿Quién mató a Palomino Molero?</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/Who_Killed_Palomino_Molero%3F" title="Who Killed Palomino Molero?">Who Killed Palomino Molero?</a></i>, 1987)</li>
<li>1987 – <i>El hablador</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Storyteller_(Vargas_Llosa_novel)" title="The Storyteller (Vargas Llosa novel)">The Storyteller</a></i>, 1989)</li>
<li>1988 – <i>Elogio de la madrastra</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/In_Praise_of_the_Stepmother" title="In Praise of the Stepmother">In Praise of the Stepmother</a></i>, 1990)</li>
<li>1993 – <i>Lituma en los Andes</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/Death_in_the_Andes" title="Death in the Andes">Death in the Andes</a></i>, 1996)</li>
<li>1997 – <i>Los cuadernos de don Rigoberto</i> (<i>The Notebooks of Don Rigoberto</i>, 1998)</li>
<li>2000 – <i>La fiesta del chivo</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Feast_of_the_Goat" title="The Feast of the Goat">The Feast of the Goat</a></i>, 2001)</li>
<li>2003 – <i>El paraíso en la otra esquina</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Way_to_Paradise" title="The Way to Paradise">The Way to Paradise</a></i>, 2003)</li>
<li>2006 – <i>Travesuras de la niña mala</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Bad_Girl" title="The Bad Girl">The Bad Girl</a></i>, 2007)</li>
<li>2010 – <i>El sueño del celta</i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Dream_of_the_Celt" title="The Dream of the Celt">The Dream of the Celt</a></i>, 2010)</li>
<li>2013 – <i>El héroe discreto</i> (<i>The Discreet Hero</i>, 2015)</li>
<li>2016 – <i>Cinco esquinas</i> (<i>The Neighborhood</i>, 2018)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-fiction">Non-fiction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mario_Vargas_Llosa&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Non-fiction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>1958 – <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Bases_para_una_interpretaci%C3%B3n_de_Rub%C3%A9n_Dar%C3%ADo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Bases para una interpretación de Rubén Darío (page does not exist)">Bases para una interpretación de Rubén Darío</a></i> (<i><a href="/w/index.php?title=The_basis_for_interpretation_of_Ruben_Dario&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="The basis for interpretation of Ruben Dario (page does not exist)">The basis for interpretation of Ruben Dario</a></i>)</li>
<li>1971 – <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Garc%C3%ADa_M%C3%A1rquez:_historia_de_un_deicidio&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="García Márquez: historia de un deicidio (page does not exist)">García Márquez: historia de un deicidio</a></i> (<i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Garc%C3%ADa_M%C3%A1rquez:_Story_of_a_Deicide&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="García Márquez: Story of a Deicide (page does not exist)">García Márquez: Story of a Deicide</a></i>)</li>
<li>1975 – <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=La_org%C3%ADa_perpetua:_Flaubert_y_%22Madame_Bovary%22&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="La orgía perpetua: Flaubert y &quot;Madame Bovary&quot; (page does not exist)">La orgía perpetua: Flaubert y "Madame Bovary"</a></i> (<i><a href="/wiki/The_Perpetual_Orgy" title="The Perpetual Orgy">The Perpetual Orgy</a></i>)</li>
<li>1983 – <i><a href="/wiki/Contra_viento_y_marea" title="Contra viento y marea">Contra viento y marea</a></i> vol. 1 (<i>Making Waves</i>) – the English translation has selections from all three volumes of <i>Contra viento y marea</i></li>

<li>1990 – <i><a href="/wiki/Contra_viento_y_marea" title="Contra viento y marea">Contra viento y marea</a></i> vol. 3</li>
<li>1990 – <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=La_verdad_de_las_mentiras:_ensayos_sobre_la_novela_moderna&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="La verdad de las mentiras: ensayos sobre la novela moderna (page does not exist)">La verdad de las mentiras: ensayos sobre la novela moderna</a></i> (<i><a href="/w/index.php?title=A_Writer%27s_Reality&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="A Writer&#39;s Reality (page does not exist)">A Writer's Reality</a></i>)</li>
<li>1993 – <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=El_pez_en_el_agua._Memorias&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="El pez en el agua. Memorias (page does not exist)">El pez en el agua. Memorias</a></i> (<i><a href="/wiki/A_Fish_in_the_Water" title="A Fish in the Water">A Fish in the Water</a></i>)</li>

<li>1996 – <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=La_utop%C3%ADa_arcaica:_Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Arguedas_y_las_ficciones_del_indigenismo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="La utopía arcaica: José María Arguedas y las ficciones del indigenismo (page does not exist)">La utopía arcaica: José María Arguedas y las ficciones del indigenismo</a></i> (<i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Archaic_utopia:_Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Arguedas_and_the_fictions_of_indigenismo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Archaic utopia: José María Arguedas and the fictions of indigenismo (page does not exist)">Archaic utopia: José María Arguedas and the fictions of indigenismo</a></i>)</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Drama">Drama</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mario_Vargas_Llosa&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Drama">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>1952 – <i>La huida del inca</i></li>
<li>1981 – <i>La señorita de Tacna</i></li>
<li>1983 – <i>Kathie y el hipopótamo</i></li>
<li>1986 – <i>La Chunga</i></li>
<li>1993 – <i>El loco de los balcones</i></li>
<li>1996 – <i>Ojos bonitos, cuadros feos</i></li>
<li>2007 – <i>Odiseo y Penélope</i></li>
<li>2008 – <i>Al pie del Támesis</i></li>
<li>2010 – <i>Las mil y una noches</i></li></ul>
</div>
<p>Vargas Llosa's essays and journalism have been collected as <i>Contra viento y marea</i>, issued in three volumes (1983, 1986, and 1990). A selection has been edited by John King and translated and published as <i>Making Waves</i>.
</p>
<ul><li>2003 – "The Language of Passion"</li></ul>
